faithfully calling thee thou hast appointed mediator betweene thee wretched man christ jesus righteous humbly acknowledge nothing selfe present unto thy majestie confession mine owne vilenesse nothing sinfull flesh corruption matter severe judgement thee art god pure eies argument terrour despaire selfe impure sinne conceived borne child wrath disobedience whole life hath abounded bringeth forth fruit unto death done good thy sanctifying spirit made willing doe evill would done rendred unto thee according thy goodnesse would summe sin much exceed number heart faileth mee conscience telleth wilfull neglect thy service disobedience thy word concluding whole life better sinfull many way offended thee observed thou knowest many failing though spirituall blindnesse carnall security observed might judge condemne selfe thereby prevent thy severe judgement shall yet meanes escape thy strict examination lord doe humbly beg thy pardon condemne selfe renounce confidence world plead thy mercy merit thy sonne jesus justification lord looke upon thou art well pleased nothing past future thy eternall wisdome▪ look therefore bleeding wound vaine dye let thy justice satisfied obedience suffering sin lord seeing according thy sentence mankind time departure hence draweth high humbly acknowledge fraile condition due wage sinne brought mortality world thou didst put thine owne image hast made short life thou givest unto beast perish thou hast need miserie advantage destruction could inestimable price redemption blood thy holy sonne jesus given thou wouldst perish eternally must surely live resurrection life christ jesus died lord therefore seale redemption afflicted heart bride neere send holy comforter faith assurance thy mercy adorne temple lift everlasting doores soule king glory lord life may come change vaine love world love heaven change vile body may like glorious body let hence forth live life mine assured thereby repaire mine inward man joyfull resurrection life glory may life death advantage full confidence union interest may willing bee dissolved may holy saviour hast death abolished death power thereof take carnall feare bringing life immortality light unto conscience thou hast thy hand keyes death hell restraine tempter malice mischievous charge sinnewounded soule make faithfull unto death assure mee crowne righteousnesse laid love thy appearing raise life grace second death may touch mee though thou bring fraile flesh dust earth yet let death dominion though must appointed time separate soule decaying tabernacle clay let neither life death thing present future seperate soule thee thy christ acknowledge thy mercy justly mightest taken away sin sodaine untimely death set sinne sonne death condition horrour restlesse conscience bitternesse spirit seeke death cannot finde good god whose eye upon feare thee deliver soules death whose hand issue thereof seeing thou hast thus long spared accomplish thy mercy thou god ever guide unto end comfort end heart trembleth terrours death fallne upon give long expected fruit hope proposed thy word▪ blessed jesus art death death shew thy selfe saviour take afflicted soule sting death assure victory loose paine allay feare sorrowes sweeten bitternesse death untill enjoying thy presence swallowed victory holy saviour hast experience misery sin wi • hout sin hast admitted u baptized similitude thy death resurrection let feele languishing soule power thereof christ whose humane soule thy passion redemption heavy death mercifully consider infirmitie going way flesh give invincible faith thee gate hell may never prevaile speake peace comfort poore soule thou powredst thy soule death receive wearied spirit eternall life let fearefull passage bitter mee bee thou ever present suffering holy ghost comforter elect leave comfortlesse let gathered father peace bring life wherein thou hast promised wipe away teares eye shall bee death sorrow paine bitter effect sinne lord heare lord despisest broken contrite heart mercy upon lord receive petition appointed houre come lord jesus saviour redeemer deliver bondage corruption lord consider doe lord come quickly even come lord jesus amen 1 tim 1 17 unto king eternall imortall invisible wise god honour glory ever ever • amen finis march 23 1649 perusing treatise entituled guide holy city found every way learned judicious
